           <script>
            // Update
 
 function update() {
 
 
 
 var arr = $('#Arrival').datepicker().val()
 var parts = arr.split("-");
 var oldDate=  new Date(parts[0],parts[1]-1 , parts[2], 12, 00, 0, 0) ;
 var countdays = 7;
 var ms = oldDate.getTime() + (86400000 * countdays);
 var newDate = new Date(ms);
 
 $('#Departure').datepicker().val(newDate.toISOString().slice(0,10)); 
 
 
 }
 
 
 head.ready(function() {
 
 
 $('#submitForm').click(function() {
 		$('#schnellanfrage').submit();
 	});
 
 var date = new Date();
 var today = new Date(date.getFullYear(), date.getMonth(), date.getDate());
 var end = new Date(date.getFullYear(), date.getMonth(), date.getDate() + 7);
 
 
 
 
 
 $('#Arrival').datepicker({
 format: "yyyy-mm-dd",
 todayHighlight: true,
 startDate: today,
 endDate: end,
 autoclose: true
 });
 
 $('#Departure').datepicker({
 format: "yyyy-mm-dd",
 todayHighlight: true,
 startDate: today,
 endDate: 0,
 autoclose: true
 });
 
 $('#Arrival').datepicker('setDate', today);
 $('#Departure').datepicker('setDate', end);
 
 
 $('#datepicker1').datepicker({
 	format: "yyyy-mm-dd",
 language: "de",
  	//language: "de",
 	autoclose: true
 
 });
 
 $('#datepicker2').datepicker({
 	format: "yyyy-mm-dd",
  	//language: "de",
 language: "de",
 	autoclose: true
 });
 
 
 $( "#Arrival" ).change(function() {
   // Check input( $( this ).val() ) for validity here
  update();
 });
 
 
 
 
 //INIT
 notify();
 
 var saveString = $( "#Arrival" ).val();
 $( "#Arrival" ).on( "change", function() {
 	setInterval(function(){ 
 	checkField();
 	}, 1000);	
 } );
 
 $( "#Departure" ).on( "change", function() {
   notify();
 } );
 function checkField() {
   if (saveString != $( "#Arrival" ).val()) {
     notify();
     clearInterval();
   }
 }
 });
 
 var monthNames = [ "Januar", "Februar", "M\u00e4rz", "April", "Mai", "Juni",
         "Juli", "August", "September", "Oktober", "November", "Dezember" ];
 
 
 function notify() {
       var dateString = $( "#Arrival" ).val();
       var parts = dateString.split("-");
       var d = new Date(parts[0], parts[1]-1, parts[2],12,0,0,0);
       $("#field-arrival-month").html(monthNames [d.getMonth()]);
       $("#field-arrival-day").html(d.getDate());
 
       var dateStringDept = $( "#Departure" ).val();
       var partsDept = dateStringDept.split("-");
       var ddept = new Date(partsDept[0], partsDept[1]-1, partsDept[2],12,0,0,0);
       $("#field-departure-month").html(monthNames [ddept.getMonth()]);
       $("#field-departure-day").html(ddept.getDate());
 }
           </script>
